        const API_END_POINT = "https://dataapi.moc.go.th/";
        var getUrlParameter = function getUrlParameter(sParam) {
            var sPageURL = window.location.search.substring(1),
                sURLVariables = sPageURL.split('&'),
                sParameterName,
                i;

            for (i = 0; i < sURLVariables.length; i++) {
                sParameterName = sURLVariables[i].split('=');

                if (sParameterName[0] === sParam) {
                    return sParameterName[1] === undefined ? true : decodeURIComponent(sParameterName[1]);
                }
            }
        };

/**/</script>

<script>
    function sendApiData() {
        var api_endpoint = API_END_POINT + "gis-product-prices?product_id=" + $("#product_id").val() + "&from_date=" + $("#from_date").val() + "&to_date=" + $("#to_date").val();$("#api_endpoint").html(api_endpoint);$.get(api_endpoint, function (data) {
            console.log(data);
            $("pre").fadeIn();
            $(".json").html(JSON.stringify(data, null, 4));
        });

    }
</script>

    <script>
        function scrollToTop() {
            $('html,body').animate({
                scrollTop: 0
            }, 'slow');
            $('.backtotop').fadeOut();

        }
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(window).scroll(function () {
                if ($('body').height() <= ($(window).height() + $(window).scrollTop())) {
                    $('.backtotop').fadeIn();
                } else {
                    $('.backtotop').fadeOut();


                }
            });


        });
        $(document).ready(function () {
            $("select:not(.no-add)").select2({
                tags: "true",
                placeholder: {
                    id: "-1",
                    text: "",
                },
                allowClear: true,
                width: '100%',
                createTag: function (params) {
                    var term = $.trim(params.term);

                    if (term === '') {
                        return null;
                    }

                    return {
                        id: term,
                        text: term,
                        value: true // add additional parameters
                    }
                }
            });
            $(".no-add").select2({
                placeholder: {
                    id: "-1",
                    text: "",
                },
                allowClear: true,
                width: '100%',
            });
        });

        function exportAsExcel() {
            $('input[name=task]').val('export_excel');
            $('#search-form').submit();
            $('input[name=task]').val('search');
        }

        function exportAsPDF() {
            $('input[name=task]').val('export_pdf');
            $('#search-form').submit();
            $('input[name=task]').val('search');
        }

        function exportAsCSV() {
            $('input[name=task]').val('export_csv');
            $('#search-form').submit();
            $('input[name=task]').val('search');
        }

        function clearSearchForm() {
            $('#search-form input[type!="hidden"]').val("");
            $('#search-form select').val("").trigger("change");

        }
        function showPopup(id) {
            var chart = $("#" + id);
            var modal = $(".modal-body");
            //var shade = $("<div>").addClass("shade").appendTo(modal).on("click", close);
            var placeholder = $("<div>").prop("id", id + "_placeholder").hide().insertBefore(chart);
            // $(document.body).append(modal);

            modal.html("");
            chart.appendTo(modal).addClass("chart").removeClass("boxshadow");

            $("#myModal").on("hidden.bs.modal", function () {
                // put your default event here
                chart.insertAfter(placeholder).removeClass("chart").addClass("boxshadow");
            });

        }

        function toggleIcon(e) {
            $(e.target)
                .prev('.card-header')
                .find(".fa")
                .toggleClass('fa-chevron-circle-up fa-chevron-circle-down');
        }
        if ($('.accordion').length) {
            $('.accordion').on('hidden.bs.collapse', toggleIcon);
            $('.accordion').on('shown.bs.collapse', toggleIcon);
        }

    </script>

    

    

</body>
</html>
